#	Fixed Asset Investent - Dimension other (197) would qualify as being Financial Assets within defintions of FRS 13 and FRS 25.
#	They would match back to FI - Primary - Asset - Categories a) Held to Maturity Investments and b) Available for Sale Financial Assets. But both these categories have a Current and Non Current dimension.
#	So any check, whether in BROs or RG needs to isolate FAI Dim FAIHoldings.Others (197). Then further isolate FinInstrCurrentNonCurrent.NonCurrent (240) to show as Fixed or FinInstrCurrentNonCurrent.Current (241) to show as Current.
